<S n="601">
<s>arTA gfhe nivartante SmaSAne cEva bAnDavAH .</s>
<s>sukftaM duzkftaM cApi gacCantamanugacCati ..</s>
</S>
<D n="601">
<b>601.</b> Die Reichthümer bleiben im Hause
und die Angehörigen kehren auf der
Leichenstätte um; die guten und bösen
Werke aber folgen dir nach auf deinem
Wege zum Jenseits.
</D>
<F n="601">
601) SUBHĀṢ. 86. Vgl. Spruch <s>A
SmaSAnAnnivartante</s> und <s>mftaM
SarIramutsfjya</s>.
</F>
<V3 n="601">
601. = NĪTIŚĀSTRA in
Telugu-Charr. 74. CARR. 377. ²b. <s>mitra</s>
st.<s>cEva</s> an beiden Stellen. ²c.
<s>cEva</s> st. <s>cApi</s> an beiden
Stellen.
</V3>
</entry>

<entry>
<info L="602" page="1.111" gtypes="S,D,F,V3,V5"/>
<S n="602">
<s>arTAturARAM na gururna banDuH kAmAturARAM na BayaM na lajjA .</s>
<s>cintAturARAM na suKaM na nidrA kzuDAturARAM na balaM na budDiH ..</s>
<pb n="1.112"/>
</S>
<D n="602" a="3597">
<b>602.</b> (<b>3597.</b>) Von Geld Gequälte haben
keinen Vater und keinen Freund, von
Liebe Gequälte keine Furcht und keine
Scham, von Sorgen Gequälte keine Freude
und keinen Schlaf, von Hunger Gequälte
keine Kraft und keinen Verstand.
</D>
<F n="602">
602) VIKRAMAC. 132. Der Schluss von
²c. ist in der Hdschr. verwischt, war
aber von ROTH, wie die Ausg. in
Telugu-Schrift zeigt, richtig
hergestellt worden. ²d. <s>na rucirna
kAlaH</s> die Ausg.
</F>
<V3 n="602">
602. = NĪTIŚĀSTRA in
Telugu-Charr. 15. CARR 377. ²c.
<s>vidyAturARAM</s> (besser) an beiden
Stellen. ²d. <s>na rucirna pakvam</s> st.
<s>na balaM na budDiH</s> an beiden
Stellen.
</V3>
<V5 n="602">
-- 602. SPHUṬAŚLOKA. ²c. <s>vidyAturARAM</s>. ²d. <s>na rucirna velA</s>.
</V5>

<D n="603" a="3598">
<b>603.</b> (<b>3598.</b>) Reichthümer aufzugeben

Mühe; darum soll man sich über ihren
Verlust keine Sorgen machen.

<info L="606" page="1.112" gtypes="S,D,F,V1,V3,V4"/>
<S n="606">
<s>arTAnAmISize tvaM vayamapi ca girAmISmahe yAvaditTaM</s>
<s>SUrastvaM vAdidarpajvaraSamanaviDAvakzayaM pAwavaM naH .</s>
<s>sevante tvAM DanAnDA matimalahataye mAmapi SrotukAmA</s>
<s>mayyapyAsTA na te cettvayi mama sutarAmeza rAjangato 'smi ..</s>
<pb n="1.113"/>
</S>
<D n="606" a="220">
<b>606.</b> (<b>220.</b>) Du gebietest über
Reichthümer, wir gebieten über Reden je
nach Bedürfniss; du bist ein Kriegsheld,
wir besitzen eine unverwüstliche
Geschicklichkeit im Besänftigen des
Uebermuthsfiebers der Worthelden; dir
huldigen durch Reichthümer Verblendete,
mir solche, die gern das Ohr leihen, um
die Geistesschlacken abzustossen; machst
du dir auch Nichts aus mir, so mache ich
mir doch gar viel aus dir; da habe ich
mich, o Fürst, schon davongemacht.
</D>
<F n="606">
606) BHARTṚ. ed. BOHL. HAEB. und
lith. Ausg. III 3, 53. lith. Ausg. I 44.
lith. Ausg. II 30. GALAN. 49.

vyavahArAvicari kfte satIti BAvaH</s>
Comm. in der lith. Ausg. II). ²b.
<s>vAgmi</s> und <s>vADi</s> st. <s>vAdi;
darpanyupaSamana, pAravaM; pAwavantaH</s>
st. <s>pAwavaM naH; te</s> st. <s>naH</s>. ²c.
<s>DanAQyA; iha</s> st. <s>api</s>. ²d.

<D n="615" a="225">
<b>615.</b> (<b>225.</b>) Der Bedürftige geniesst
kein Ansehen, der Hochgestiegene fällt,
der Verliebte zieht sich einen
Spitznamen zu, der Habsüchtige bedeckt
sich mit Unehre, wer nicht kämpft, wird
geringgeachtet, der Böse hat seine
Freude an den Fehlern Anderer, der
Besitzlose betrügt, der Aufgeregte ist
nicht bei vollem Bewusstsein, der
Betrübte ist in Besorgniss, wer Böses
den Leuten nachredet, macht sich
verhasst, der Spieler geräth immer und
immer wieder in Noth.
</D>

des stattlichen Hauses verbracht hat,
will er, der am Weinrausch Gefallen
findende Unglückliche, jetzt, da sich
ein unerträglicher Durst eingestellt
hat, nicht aus dem Kruge das
Herbstwasser trinken, welches ihm die
schlaffen Arm-Lianen der vom Minnespiel
erschöpften Geliebten darreichen,
Wasser, dessen Strahl durchsichtig wie
der Mond ist.

Blättern dieser Blume sass, begab sich
nach dem Willen des Schicksals an einen
andern Ort und findet jetzt grossen
Gefallen am Saft der Kuṭaja-Blüthe
(Wrightia antidysenterica R. Br.).
</D>
<F n="645">
645) VṚDDHA-CĀṆ. 15, 15.
</F>

fleischfressende Wesen.

Feuergottes, die Gesammtheit der Wesen
eine Erscheinungsform der Weltseele.

<D n="968">

herabwirft; ein Kalb ist rein beim

<S n="993">
<s>AyuH kallolalolaM katipayadivasasTAyinI yOvanaSrI-</s>

</S>
<D n="993" a="376">
<b>993.</b> (<b>376.</b>) Das Leben ist unstät wie
eine Welle, der Jugend Herrlichkeit
währt nur wenige Tage, die Reichthümer
kommen und gehen wie die Gedanken, die
grosse Schaar der Sinnesgenüsse ist wie
das Zucken der Blitze in der Regenzeit,
und wenn euch die Geliebte umschlingt
und an's Herz drückt, so dauert auch
dieses nicht lange: heftet euren Sinn
auf das Brahman, damit ihr über ein Meer
von Gefahren, die Welt, glücklich
hinübergelanget.
</D>

<D n="996" a="378">
<b>996.</b> (<b>378.</b>) Der Menschen Leben ist auf
hundert Jahre abgemessen; die Hälfte
davon geht in Nacht (im Schlafe) dahin,
die eine Hälfte der anderen Hälfte in
Kindheit und Greisenalter, die übrig
bleibende wird unter Krankheit, Trennung
und Schmerz im Dienst und Aehnlichem
verbracht. Wie können die Menschen
Freude haben an einem Leben, das den
Blasen einer Wasserwoge gleicht?
</D>

<D n="997">
<b>997.</b> Das Leben fährt wie der Wind
dahin, Macht ist wie ein Regenbogen von
kurzer Dauer, Jugend ist wie ein Blitz

wie die Wellen eines Gebirgsflusses,
Jugendfrische klappt wie Elephantenohren
rasch zusammen, der Leib wird von
Krankheiten heimgesucht: habt ihr alles
dieses erkannt, so übet Gutes, das
lauter ist und stets beharrt.
</D>
